<h1 class="header"> <span class="itemprop" itemprop="name">Stephen Fry</span>
<span>(I)</span>
</h1>
<div class="infobar" id="name-job-categories">

<div class="txt-block" id="name-bio-text">
<div class="name-trivia-bio-text">
<div class="inline" itemprop="description">
Writer, actor, comedian, doer of good works, excellent good friend to the famous and not, Fry lives in his London SW1 flat and his Norfolk house when not traveling. Famous for his public declaration of celibacy in the "Tatler" back in the 1980s, <a href="/name/nm0000668?ref_=nm_ov_bio_lk1">Emma Thompson</a> has characterised her friend as "90 percent gay, 10 percent other." Stephen Fry was born ...            <span class="see-more inline nobr-only">
<a href="/name/nm0000410/bio?ref_=nm_ov_bio_sm">See full bio</a> »
            </span>
</div> </div>
</div>
<div class="txt-block" id="name-born-info">

<time datetime="1957-8-24" itemprop="birthDate">
<a href="/search/name?birth_monthday=8-24&amp;refine=birth_monthday&amp;ref_=nm_ov_bth_monthday">August 24</a>, 
     
<a href="/search/name?birth_year=1957&amp;ref_=nm_ov_bth_year">1957</a>
</time>
            in
            <a href="/search/name?birth_place=Hampstead%2C+London%2C+England%2C+UK&amp;ref_=nm_ov_bth_place">Hampstead, London, England, UK</a>
</div>
</td>

                consoleLog('Pixel failure ' + e.toString(),'sis');
            }
            if (window.ueLogError) { 
                window.ueLogError(e);
            }
        }
    }, 20);
</script>
<!-- End SIS code -->
